BALTIC OPERATIONAL AND OCEANOGRAPHICAL SYSTEM (BOOS)
OCEANOGRAPHIC DATA
STATIONS

BOOSNR	= Station Number used in BOOS
PLATFORM	= Platform ID
STATION	= Station Name (Vessel Name)
LAT	= Latitude in decimal degress
LON	= Longitude in decimal degress
 
TYPE	= Station Type
where
FP	= Fixed Platform
TG	= Tide Gauge
MB	= Moored Buoy
FB	= Ferrybox/Vessel
GL	= Glider
CT	= CTD Profiles 
SF	= Lightship

DATUM	= Sea Level Reference Datum

OWNER/PROVIDER/PU = Station Owner / Data Provider / Production unit
where
